## Executive Summary

Comprehensive read-only mapping-integrity audit of all ACTIVE form templates in `harbaugh-forms-dev`, restarted after an interrupted Cursor session (power outage) and completed from an independently verified clean state on 2026-07-21.

- **17 ACTIVE forms**, **869 ACTIVE mappings**, **68 PDF pages containing mappings — every page rendered and visually inspected** with mapping overlays against the current stored PDFs.
- **Headline finding: the two disputed Listing Agreement mappings are VALID.** `OTHER_FEES_REIMBURSABLE_EXPENSES` (TXR-1101 p3, ¶5E(3)) and `KNOWN_DISTRICTS` (TXR-1101 p8, ¶12K) each land exactly on a real, visible, writable continuation blank line on the current TXR-1101 (01-05-26) PDF. Lee's report that neither appears visibly on the PDF is contradicted by direct rendering; the likely source of the report is a **data-model defect, not a PDF defect**: both fields (and 17 others) have `source_path = null`, which silently breaks automatic value resolution in the packet UI while the PDF blank itself is fine.
- **Classification totals: 793 V1 (visually verified), 75 V2 (valid location, tight placement needing precision confirmation), 1 R7 (mapping to an INACTIVE catalog field), 0 R1/R2/R3/R4/R5/R6/U.** *(Update 2026-07-21: the single R7 was resolved by reactivating the accidentally inactivated catalog field — see High-Risk Mappings below. The 75 V2 items remain open cosmetic notes.)*
- **No geometry defects**: no off-page, zero-size, or wrong-page mappings. All duplicate-coordinate/multi-mapping cases are intentional running headers.
- **No historical-version orphans**: every current PDF was uploaded before its mappings were created/adjusted and has not been replaced since (only a storage-path rename on 7/13–14), so no mapping refers to an older PDF version.
- **19 mappings have a null `source_path`** where automatic resolution is expected (17 on TXR-1101, 1 on TXR-1405, 1 on TXR-1102). All are visually valid placements; the defect is data-model-side only.
- **No database, repository, PDF, or configuration changes** were made by this audit or by the interrupted session.

## Interrupted Session Recovery

- **Repository state found:** `main` checked out at `d9a9f0fa1e516608b515056ad2241eef5d537709`, identical to `origin/main`; working tree clean; no staged files, stash entries, extra branches, or new commits; reflog shows no reset/merge/rebase/cherry-pick/amend during the outage window.
- **Running processes found:** only the legitimate Next.js dev server (`npm run dev`), restarted ~9:05 AM after the machine rebooted. No orphaned test runners, Supabase CLI, migration, PDF, or audit processes. Nothing was writing to the database or generating files.
- **Git operations found:** none. No `MERGE_HEAD`, `CHERRY_PICK_HEAD`, `REVERT_HEAD`, `rebase-merge`/`rebase-apply` directories, and no stale `index.lock`.
- **Partial files found:** none. The interrupted run (≈9:06–9:11 AM) executed only read-only git commands and file reads before power loss; no `MAPPING_INTEGRITY_AUDIT.md`, temp JSON/SQL, screenshots, or audit scripts existed. A handful of files showed 9:05–9:06 AM filesystem timestamps, attributable to the dev-server restart; `git status`/`git diff` confirmed contents unchanged.
- **Database changes found:** none in the interrupted window. All recent writes date to the documented 7/20 defaults-restoration session. Integrity spot-checks all passed: global catalog preference literals = 0; Lee legacy all-forms Private defaults = 56 ACTIVE; Lee form-specific Private defaults = 19 ACTIVE; Organization defaults = 4 ACTIVE; no duplicate ACTIVE logical defaults; the accidental `buyer_client_name_1` test row remains soft-deleted; the two disputed Listing mappings are byte-identical to their pre-outage values.
- **Configuration/deployment:** `.env.local` targets Supabase project `ewxsxwzezhkeawnjvigx` (harbaugh-forms-dev) only; no production URL/project present; no env files modified; no deployments; no migrations applied (fully or partially); no credentials written into any audit artifact.
- **Cleanup/quarantine performed:** nothing required quarantine, so `_interrupted_audit_recovery/` was not created. The restarted audit used a fresh untracked `_audit_tmp/` working directory (read-only scripts, DB dumps, downloaded PDFs, page renders), removed at completion.
- **Why the restarted audit can be trusted:** every prior assumption was re-derived from scratch — repository state from git itself, database state from fresh read-only dumps, PDF truth from freshly downloaded copies of the stored templates, and placement verdicts from direct rendering rather than cached conclusions.

## Disputed Listing Agreement Mappings

Both disputed TXR-1101 mappings are **valid on the current PDF**. Full reconstruction:

### OTHER_FEES_REIMBURSABLE_EXPENSES (TXR-1101 p3)
1. **Concept in current wording?** Yes — ¶5E(3): "Other Fees and/or Reimbursable Expenses: ______".
2. **Writable blank?** Yes — a full-width continuation blank line under ¶5E(3).
3. **Where do coordinates land?** x≈90.6, y≈494.5 on page 3 — exactly on that continuation blank (zoom-verified render).
4. **Paragraph-estimated?** Originally yes (migration `20250622220000`, note "paragraph-based estimated placement"), then manually repositioned in the mapping editor on 6/29 15:49 (fractional coordinates, update timestamp).
5. **Existed on an earlier TXR-1101?** Only one TXR-1101 PDF has ever been stored (uploaded 6/16/2026, version 01-05-26); there is no earlier in-system version.
6. **Copied during a PDF replacement?** No — the PDF was never replaced; only its storage path was renamed on 7/13–14.
7. **Details-table column?** Yes — `listing_agreement_details.other_fees_reimbursable_expenses` (migration `20250622200000`).
8. **Packet usage?** Yes — 2 ACTIVE packet instances, both nonblank ("NA").
9. **Data-model-only?** No — a real writable blank exists.
10. **Recommended action:** Preserve the mapping. Fix the data-model defect: the catalog field's `source_path` is null (lost during catalog dedup — the uppercase-key field row created 6/24 never received the lowercase seed's `source_path`), so automatic resolution from `listing_agreement_details` silently fails and the packet UI shows the field as unresolved — the most plausible origin of Lee's "not visible" report. Restore `source_path = 'other_fees_reimbursable_expenses'` (a separate write task, not performed by this audit).

### KNOWN_DISTRICTS (TXR-1101 p8)
1. **Concept in current wording?** Yes — ¶12K districts disclosure: "(list all that Seller is aware of): ______".
2. **Writable blank?** Yes — a full-width continuation blank line in ¶12K.
3. **Where do coordinates land?** x≈73.7, y≈280.8 on page 8 — exactly on that continuation blank (zoom-verified render).
4. **Paragraph-estimated?** Originally yes (same migration; the earlier INACTIVE seed even sat on the wrong page, 7 vs 8), then manually repositioned in the mapping editor on 6/29 16:08.
5. **Existed on an earlier TXR-1101?** No earlier in-system PDF version exists.
6. **Copied during a PDF replacement?** No — no replacement occurred.
7. **Details-table column?** Yes — `listing_agreement_details.known_districts`.
8. **Packet usage?** Yes — 2 ACTIVE packet instances, both nonblank ("NA").
9. **Data-model-only?** No.
10. **Recommended action:** Preserve the mapping; restore `source_path = 'known_districts'` for auto-resolution; ask Lee to re-check in the packet UI after the fix.

Notes per form (from full visual inspection of every mapped page):

- **TXR-1101 (7, Listing Agreement, 11 pages):** all 104 mappings land on real blanks/checkboxes; the 10 repeated `PROPERTY_FULL_ADDRESS` header boxes are narrower than the printed blank and sit slightly left — functional, flagged V2 for precision only. 17 mappings have null `source_path` (data-model defect, placements fine).
- **TXR-1601 (11, 1-4 Family Resale Contract, 12 pages):** 173 mappings; all placements correct. 32 V2s are tight placements slightly overlapping printed text (earnest money/escrow agent cluster on p2, survey/title cluster on p3, running header on every page).
- **TXR-2001 (18, Residential Lease, 16 pages):** 140 mappings all on real blanks/boxes; none has ever been used in a packet (form appears not yet used in production) — risk signal only.
- **TXR-1102 (15, Lease Listing, 11 pages):** 159 mappings, all correct; 1 null source path (`LEASE_SCHEDULING_COMPANY`).
- **TXR-1901 (17, Third-Party Financing Addendum, AcroForm):** 61 mappings matched to genuine AcroForm widgets by `pdf_field_name`; 6 V2s where the drawn rect overlaps neighboring widget text — values fill via the widget, so low risk.
- **TXR-1501 (1, Buyer Rep, 6 pages):** all placements correct; contains the single R7 (see above).
- **TXR-1404 (13), TXR-1903 (14), TXR-1423 (16), TXR-1922 (12), TXR-1405 (8), TXR-2501 (3), TXR-2516 (5), TXR-2517 (6), TXR-1906 (9), TXR-1401 (21 & 23):** single-page forms/addenda; all placements verified on real blanks/checkboxes. Forms 21/23 share the condo-addendum template; their single header-address mapping covers the left half of the blank (V2 precision note).

## Geometry Findings

- All 869 ACTIVE mappings reference existing pages, sit fully within page bounds, and have positive, plausible sizes. **Zero off-page, partially off-page, zero-size, implausibly small/large, or wrong-page mappings.**
- Duplicate/overlapping coordinates and multi-mapping-same-field cases (e.g. `property_concerning_full_address` ×11 on TXR-1601, `PROPERTY_FULL_ADDRESS` ×10 on TXR-1101) are **intentional running headers**, one per page.
- Minor precision issues (not defects): header address boxes narrower than the printed blank (TXR-1101, TXR-1401), tight overlaps against printed labels on dense contract pages (TXR-1601 p2/p3, TXR-2001 p1). These are the 75 V2 rows.

## Historical-Version Findings

- Every ACTIVE form's stored PDF predates its mappings' creation/last adjustment and has never been replaced. The 7/13–14 storage-path migration renamed object paths only (byte-identical files). **No mapping exists only on an older PDF version (0 R2).**
- TXR-1101 lineage: concepts added to `listing_agreement_details` (`20250622200000`); catalog seeded with lowercase keys + source paths (`20250622210000`); paragraph-estimated mappings inserted then refined (`20250622220000`, `20250622230000`). On 6/24/2026 an uppercase-key generation of catalog fields was created without `source_path`; the `20250622250000` packet-instance backfill also set `source_path = null` where it back-filled `source_type`. Net effect: 19 ACTIVE fields expected to auto-resolve have null `source_path`. The 7/17 `clear_all_global_catalog_defaults` migration did **not** touch `source_path`.
- Several migration-seeded placements were later hand-tuned in the mapping editor (fractional coordinates, 6/29 update timestamps) against the same PDFs still in use — so the "paragraph-estimated" notes in `notes` overstate current placement uncertainty.

## Packet-Usage Findings

- 591 of 869 mappings (68%) have at least one packet field instance; **278 have never been used** — concentrated in not-yet-used forms: TXR-2001 (140), TXR-1903 (38), TXR-1423 (37), TXR-1404 (27), TXR-1405 (20), TXR-1922 (15), TXR-1401 form 23 (1). Zero use is a risk signal only; placements were visually verified regardless.
- Both disputed mappings: 2 ACTIVE instances each, values "NA", sources = packet/manual; the values would render correctly at the verified blanks.
- The R7 mapping (`BUYER_REP_BROKER_SGN_CHECKBOX`) has 3 instances — reviewed 2026-07-21: all three attach to the original field ID (`2a32353f…`), value `"false"`, source `empty`, non-override; they remained valid and untouched through the field's reactivation.

## Recommended Review Order

1. **R7 (1 item):** **resolved 2026-07-21** — the TXR-1501 p6 `BUYER_REP_BROKER_SGN_CHECKBOX` catalog field was reactivated as `manual_only` (migration `20260721190000`); the mapping was valid and unchanged. The original "repoint or deactivate" suggestion was wrong: the field's inactivation, not the mapping, was the defect.
2. **Null source paths (19 items):** ~~restore `source_path`~~ — **resolved 2026-07-22 for the 18 Listing fields** by migration `20260722010000_remove_obsolete_listing_details_sources.sql` (convert to `manual_only`, not restore paths), plus Lee Personal form-specific `NA` defaults for the disputed TXR-1101 pair. TXR-1405 `HOA_ASSOCIATION_ADDRESS` intent remains a separate open item. The placements themselves remain visually valid as recorded here.
3. **V2 precision items (75):** optional cosmetic pass — widen/nudge header address boxes and the tight TXR-1601/TXR-2001 money-field rects.
4. **No-packet-use forms:** no action needed; re-verify organically on first production use.
5. **V1 (793):** no action.
